mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	But put on some digested ointments, or poultices made of barley flour boiled in water and honey, until it drips.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then heal with other treatments until it is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if a bone fracture comes with the wound, and it is small, pull it out using fine tweezers.
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	Hereafter I shall tell you about fractures of the head.
de la plaie dou col	Of the neck wound
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If the wound on the neck is simple and has no distinction from that of the head, but if the nerve of the neck or the artery is cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the nerve, there is no other remedy but to leave the healing and not apply any restriction, for it harms nerves and makes them retreat.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And do not put anything cold on the wound, for the substance of nerves is cold, and its continuation is with the brain, which is the highest member.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	However, the medicine should be boiled, as clear water washed with sweet water and mixed with rose oil, and then boiled again in sweet water.
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	And other stones of similar kind should be prepared in the same way, and anointed with oil. (Note: The original text mentions "pieres," which can refer to a variety of things including minerals or rocks, but without additional context, it's hard to determine exactly what is meant here.)
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the wound is large, tie and bind it, then treat it until it heals.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and swollen with pus, pierce or make an incision lower down.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if the artery is cut, bleeding will follow, so you must stop it, tie it, and cauterize as necessary;
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	And if the spine of the throat is cut or pierced, and the windpipe guarded, so that the flesh goes,
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	If the windpipe is cut above the neck, do not touch the throat but instead reset it according to its natural shape;
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then apply traction, let it rest for some days, then heal with discarded ointments until it heals;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if the wound presses on the bone, squeeze it.
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	and if there are bone fragments, pull them out as much as you can, and those that you cannot remove, leave until the wound heals.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	make the opening even and aligned.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, sprinkle powder on it as I have said.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and it has a fistula, treat it as I have said in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of the sword or knife wound
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it is a thrust wound from a lance or knife and the wound is perforated, examine whether the wound exudes pus vents (ventosa) so that you know if the wound is mortal.
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	And if it's not complete and is fresh with all its blood, do not put the powder on it in the first hour, nor tie it for the blood that dissolves it completely.
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	And return to the heart, and cut open the patient.
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but apply attracting ointment, and tie it twice a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you don't have ointment, place thick cotton on the wound to draw out moisture.
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	And make the patient sleep on the wound for three days, or four, or more.
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	If there is no spasm, nor severe trembling of heart nor drawing of the bowels.
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	If you see good progress, know that the wound is healed.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Treat the disease and other treatments, as long as he is healthy;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	And if it cannot heal, and an abscess forms, immediately make incisions to let the pus out, and treat it as one should.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife cut, and it is simple (or deeper), on the front or back, treat the part in front of it;
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	If it is large, sew [the wound]; if it is small, apply powder; and if it is pressed into the bone, take pieces from it, whether the wound is open or the flesh torn off [by force], pull the pieces out if they are dislodged.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	And if they are not dislodged, leave the wound to drain, align the extraction [of the pieces].
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	And for other wounds on other limbs, the judgement is as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	The dislocation of the abdomen
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The dislocations of the abdomen are large, medium, and small.
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From a large wound, sometimes the intestines or the nerves of the intestines protrude due to insertion.
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	And stitching is more difficult, and sometimes a small wound is worse than a large one.
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	because if one puts them in again slowly, they are not put back in place properly.
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	because the intestines swell quickly when they feel the cold, and as a result, they enter more quickly.
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	And because the middle wound is more important, it is better to reset the intestines in their place than with the other two (large wounds).
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	And know that the rupture of the belly is according to four ways:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	the two common ruptures happen in the rupture of the abdomen,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	and the ruptures of other body parts and two other specific ruptures are common in other wounds.
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	Moreover, these are more closely related to the rupture of the abdomen, and I will explain one and clarify it.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small, and no part of the intestines protrude from it,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	and it is easy to treat, this is through one of the two ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	or because of the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or because the intestines are swollen due to cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, warm it gently: [The sentence is referring to an object or a body part which needs to be warmed up when it's cold.]
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	dampen a sponge or a thin cloth in warm water only, [The sentence suggests using warm water (damp sponge or wet cloth) to gently warm up the cold object or body part.]
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	or you cook in hot mustard and cypress and pepper. [This sentence refers to using a mixture of hot mustard (or another hot liquid), cypress, and pepper to warm up an object or body part.]
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and stir the intestines until the swelling is removed; [This sentence suggests massaging the swollen intestines in order to reduce the swelling.]
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And sometimes this wine restraining makes it move, and it is softened so that it can be opened.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the swelling separate, if the intestines are cooked with too much water or poorly cooked,
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	because in this way, the entry is closed off quickly.
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	And if it cannot enter (the joint), make a small incision with the instrument used for hemorrhoids.
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	and the first remedy is made of leeches.
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	we should not cut it unless it is absolutely necessary.
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and this is the instrument for splitting it:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	If it is cut within the hollow and does not protrude, then look at its shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is widened, and the intestines escape,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	put it back there according to its natural shape in its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	if you have the power to do so, for it is useful.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is wide, and it is in the part below the stomach.
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	Then you must make the patient lie down on their back.
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and put his legs higher than his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	And if [it is] in the part below the belly,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	lift the head and the hip higher than the parts below.
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and likewise, if the rupture of the belly is in one of the two parts.
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	align the injured part to be higher than the other.
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And thus, it is necessary to treat this as in large and small wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	In small wounds, apply what is appropriate.
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	Then take a kind and compassionate minister in your hands.
et assemble les levres;	close the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and this is the common method of stitches,
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	and you take a needle or more, according to the width of the wound,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	leave one finger's space at the head of the wound and insert a needle with one strong thread.
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	And pierce the 2 cheeks of the hide with the 2 cheeks of the knife,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is beneath the skin inside, as long as you make it pierce through that part,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and put together the 2 heads of the knife in 4 pieces.
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then tie a double thread around the needle of 2 parts,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	Then assemble the two heads of the wound together.
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and then leave one thumb's width of space, and insert another needle.
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	and tie the thread as you did for the first needle.
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and continue in this manner according to your need for the needles.
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	Until all the wound is bound;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	And let the needles be moderately thin, between fine and thick.
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	because very thin needles pierce all the skin, and very thick ones cannot enter well:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	because they should be narrowed;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and it is not good to insert the needles too deep into the flesh and skin,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	that they do not open and cut the wound before the joint.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	And then close the heads of the needles, so they do not prick the patient while sleeping.
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	and place bandages or cloths on the heads of the needles to keep them closed.
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and leave it until the wound is healed.
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	This method of stitching with needles is more suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	For him there is a needle or two. (translated from Old French to English)
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second stitching is common. (translated from Old French to English)
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	and it is that you join the two skins of leather and the two skins of silk together with a needle having one strong, middle-sized thread; (translated from Old French to English)
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	and when you have sewn all the pieces four together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	If you straighten the needle at the part where you have begun, in the manner as they customarily do with the thorns;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and put distance between each stitch, the thickness of a small egg;
ceste costure sevent li home,	this stitch binds the man,
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	I sewed a wound that one man had in his belly,
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	Who was wounded by a knife,
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	and the wound is more than one palm in size,
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	and it exposed the intestines for two palms in length.
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	and the wound was within the abdomen.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	I brought back the intestine when it had been twenty-four hours.
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	and the wound was sewn shut for fifteen days, and he cured it, and it healed.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And they had judged that he would die, and it was a miracle.
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and did not treat him with medicine because I was in one place where none could be found, nor any medicine.
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	And apply cotton wool frequently over the wound, and wash it with water of honey until it is clean.
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	I will tell you the two proper ways of sewing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle and thread it from the outer part to the inner one:
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	When it has pierced the heart straight through, place the thread's end where the tip of the needle is or where you have put the needle:
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	And make it pierced from the inside part through until the outside bends.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	And the meaning of this stitching is that you sew as pelters sew fur.
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	and that you leave the seam open once on one side, and then close it from the other, until the stitching is completely finished.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	The second method of stitching, which Galen calls specifically,
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	It is like those who put together two parts naturally.
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	and apply one of the bone ends to the other bone end in such a manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	drive an awl or bone end close to the next bone, and pierce that place only,
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	leave the two bone ends.
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	Then turn the needle, and make it pierce from the outside part to that within.
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	2 shoulders with arrows.
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	Then pierce one and the other from the outside part to that within, in 2 other shoulders with the mirror that are opposite each other.
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	and this is the common method of sewing.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	Galen said this word, and no one testifies against it.
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	one should sew the stomach with two needles, where there is thread in each.
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and one should insert one needle from one side, and the other from the other, in the manner of those who sew corsets.
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	and know that when the hernia is in the stomach,
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	The stitching is more severe than the other parts of the abdomen.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgments regarding the wound are as follows, similar to those of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	and it is that when you open the fresh wound completely with all its blood, then let the herbs move it.
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	If he reattaches the intestine and sutures it, then put powder stimulating flesh on top.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	and if it has moved (the intestine), then put any ointment that is present, until the wound heals.
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and sew the flesh, and bind the sutures, and apply the plaster.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then care for the wound as with others, until it is healed.
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	And if you have no medicine, place it immediately when it begins to emit pus, old cotton.
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	and stir it twice a day until it heals.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you have no need for other medicine in many cases when the wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	and if you doubt whether the wound might spread to the main members,
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	It is necessary that you soften thin linen in warm oil or rose oil.
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	and place it around the swellings, and beneath the armpits;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	if there is pain or purulence in the belly, which often occurs,
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	if the cleansing with black wine is hot, and similarly when the purulence reaches the intestines;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And pierce within, and know that when it is the large intestines, it is easier to heal than the small ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	The intestine called "jeun" cannot heal when perforated.
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	and it is due to the inflammation of veins therein, and the subtlety of the entire body, and the proximity of its nature to nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the hernia jumps out of the wound, replace it as you would an intestine, while it is still fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	And if it is old and has turned black or dark, you must cut away the black part, so that no blood flow comes from it.
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	For there are veins and arteries.
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	Then cut what is between the ligament.
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	And place the two shoulders hanging from the part under the wound on the side opposite the fracture to align the extraction as the splinters fall and the wound bows outwards.
de la routure dou boueil	Of the rupture of the bladder
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are torn, and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	if it can be restored in some men,
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	Because I have seen a man wounded or pierced with a lance;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	and the wound was on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	and it became inflamed and turned into a fistula, and in it were excretions and flatulence;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I treated it according to what I knew, and I did not stop subtilizing until it was healed, and the wound closed.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I see it sewed (or sutured), I suspect that the patient has pain in his stomach;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	and he had no ill-being but remained in better positions, and food and drinks;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	and some experimentalists say that when there is a small wound in the intestines, it should be tied in this manner:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	take firm twigs with large heads, then gather the lips of the wound,
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	And when the convulsion has opened the mouth, place it on the two lips,
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	so that it draws out its mouth above;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	then strike the head, and hold it until it cannot escape.
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	then place another convulsion after in this manner as before, until the wound is completely captured;
et cout la plaie.	And dress the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	If the head has become inflamed in the intestines, and brings no harm to the patient,
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	And it can be tied up the intestines with a thin thread that is cut from the intestine of an animal.
en teil maniere:	In this manner:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	take the end of this intestinal thread that is sharp and pointed.
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	then tie it to the sharp end of the thread, that is, a fine twisted flax cord.
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	then insert the thread into the awl, and sew the intestine and reset it in its place.
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	And this method of stitching fractures is not beyond the path of trust and hope;
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	If the wound is large and wide, especially if it is in one of the great intestines, there is no remedy or health, but rather subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of a fistula or
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	Know that every wound or abscess, when it matures, is universally called "fistula",
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	And likewise when it is swollen and curved.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	A fistula is like a hard, nodular thickening or swelling that does not cause pain.
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	And it is swollen like a bird's feather.
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	And sometimes clear jump, and other times thick jump;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	Sometimes thin, and other times rather thick;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	And I spoke of it in the section on wounds, that every wound which is not healed and there is no flesh,
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	is nothing but one of the eight causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	It is to know, by the small amount of blood or body.
ou por sa malice;	or for its illness.
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or because there is hard flesh within and above the lips that does not allow it to grow flesh.
ou il i a trop de bowe;	or if there is too much swelling.
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	If the loosened joint is of bad quality and torn apart,
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	if the medicine is not good in the treatment;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	because corruption is a manner of pestilence;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	because the property in the region causes slow digestion and slowness of health, and swelling by nature;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	or there are veins or bones:
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	and I have already shown all these causes, signs, and treatments of medications in sections.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	Also, I will explain to you the treatment for fistula that is made by manual work.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that a fistula occurs in all members of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	because there are fistulas that come from large veins, arteries, and nerves.
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	or to the bladder, intestines, bladder, or any of the ribs.
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	For the spine of the back or for any joint of the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	and if it comes to the property of the principal member, and similar conditions.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all fistulas that are in this way are difficult to cure, and there is only labor and ignorance.
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	and if there is any fistula that does not reach the level I have said, and you are confident in the cure,
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	And you recognize it, if you take a thorn or iron splint, if the fistula is straight, pierce it.
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	and if the fistula is twisted, seek a fine needle of wood,
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	for the wood bends with the twisting.
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	And if the fistula (an abnormal passage or connection) at the hand is pierced and you cannot find it by probing with fingers,
si la clisterize par l’un des pertus,	If the fistula by one of the wounds is
car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	because moisture is so short from one wound to another, and it cleanses (the fistula);
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont,	then seek it cautiously with your power, so that you know if there is bone or nerve in it, and whether it has penetrated to the full depth.
et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	Ask the patient carefully about the pain they feel when pressed by your hand, and the location where they feel it.
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine,	and when you know truly the location where it is, whether it is far from a joint, nerve, artery, or vein.
ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit,	or in any of the locations that I have told you, if the pain follows what I have said.
et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	and cut open the wound and the rotten flesh that is inside.
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee,	and then the cure until it heals,
et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues,	and if the fistula is properly pierced straight through, you must cut through as deeply as possible,
puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule,	then put wet tents soaked in astringent medicine at the top of the fistula,
tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	As long as the medicine corrodes the excess that remains at the bottom;
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then apply liniments of healthy fat, until it is healed;
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit,	and if it is not healed by this means, cauterize it as we have said,
et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	and if the bone is corrupted from the fistula, break it.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If vein or nerves do not obstruct or main limbs, as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee,	and if the bone is exposed, and there is decay and blackness, let it heal until all decay is removed,
puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	then cure with warm ointment until it heals;
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant,	and if not healed, make a pouch as before,
saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	Know that you are not going to the fountain:
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons,	cover it up and stay as deep as you can be.
et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	remove all the corruption, then reset its place;
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	if it is thus healed, that's good.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	If not, know that the corruption is too advanced, that you cannot reach it.
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	if there is no other remedy but to let nature take its course.
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles,	and if there is a small bone that has rotted, which you can draw out with the pliers.
si l’estrai a .i. estrument covenauble a ceu,	if it is necessary to extract it by one instrument.
et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	And if there are many bones, draw them all out, leave none of them behind.
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour,	If the moisture opposes you and there is no mistake or fear,
si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	strike and press and warm the flesh, and deliver the bones.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture,	And if you cannot remove them within an hour, place something warming on the wound.
et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os,	And let the limbs be set apart around the bones,
et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	And then the bones will have more easily.
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse,	and if it is a large bone, such as of the leg or thigh,
si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee,	hold the corruption only as long until the blackness is completely removed,
puis restoure la plaie;	Then restore the wound;
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	and if there is a large part of corruption that reaches the bone marrow;
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	it must be cut off and covered up to the corruption, and then it should be cured until it heals over.
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint .i. home en sa jambe,	I will tell you about a fistula that happened to a man in his leg;
si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	If you take example and help in your work.
Il fut .i. jovencelz entor .xxx. ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors,	A young man of about thirty years old had a pain in his leg due to something coming from within the body.
tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	The matter kept coming into the leg and it developed a large abscess, and there was no reason to open it.
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri,	But they opened it due to their foolishness until the abscesses were opened.
et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	And it becomes full of matter, and turns into a fistula, and much pus comes out that all fall down weak and wet with the body.
et maint mire i mirent cure entor .ij. ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains,	And for two years they put various remedies around it, but there was no healer skilled in the art of hands.
tant que je i fui apelez, et vi sa jambe et les medicines dont on le curoit,	until I was summoned, and I saw his leg and the medicines with which it was being treated,
et ceu que corroit par les pertus a grant cors;	And those who ran through wounds with great force;
et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	And the body of the youth became red and had a golden hue.
Je boutai une tente en l’un de ces pertus, et puis cerchai toz les pertus,	I erected a tent at one of those wounds, then searched for all the wounds.
et trovai que li uns venoit encontre l’autre de toutes les parties de la jambe.	and found that one came towards the other from all parts of the leg.
Je me hastai donques, et copai en l’un des pertus tant que je descovri une partie de l’os,	I quickly went then, and dug into one of the wounds until I discovered a part of the bone.
et le trovai corrumput et perciet, et venoit li corruption jusc’a l’os dedens;	and found it rotten and pierced through, and the corruption came to the bone within;
je soiai ceu qui m’aparissoit de l’os corrumput, et cuidai qu’il n’i eust autre corruption, fuer que celi que je ostai;	I was the one who appeared to be rotten bone, and thought there was no other corruption except that which I left.
et comensai a restourer la plaie de medicines sodans par lonc tens, et ne pot souder;	And it begins to heal the wound with salty medicines for a long time, but does not heal.
et puis rencomensai, et descovri l’os si com devant,	Then it is reopened, and the bone is exposed as before,
et trovai la corruption continuee en l’os, et la soiai, et puis l’ostai, et me penai de souder le leu;	I found continuous corruption in the bone, and I cut it out, and then I left it, and I tried to heal the wound.
mais je ne pou tant que je copai entor une palme de l’os, et le traï fuer a tout son mole,	but I could not because I covered about one palm of the bone, and it broke off in all its marrow,
puis le restourai de medicines; et il fut sanez et soudez hastanment,	Then restore it with medicine; and it heals and strengthens quickly.
et ne covint plus rencomencier l’ovraige fors por la foibleté dou malaide, qui ne pooit soffrir,	and no need to continue the work except due to the frailty of the patient, who could not endure it.
et por la paour de mort que je avoie de lui.	and because of the fear of death that I had for him.
Car por l’evacuation sanglotoit sovent, mais il fut sanez entierement,	For he often bled, but he was completely healed.
et nasquit en leu de l’os une char dure, et fut de bone disposition et n’ot point de nuisement ne de contraire dou tout en tout, ne a l’aleir ne a venir.	And in its place, a hard cyst was born on the bone, and it had good alignment and no harm or contrary effects to anything, neither in the air nor in coming.
Et se li os est brisiez en aucun leu dou cors, si le covient soier en ceste maniere:	And if the bone is broken in any part of the body, it should be done in this manner:
pren .i. liien, et l’estrain au chief de l’os qui apert,	Take one ligature and apply it to the end of the broken bone.
et comande aucun k’il l’estende en haut;	And command anyone to stretch it upwards;
et met .i. autre lien de lainne plus gros dou premier liien, et le lie sus la char qui est desor l’os,	and put another rope of heavier linen than the first one, and tie it above the skin that is detached from the bone,
et estent le chief, si que tu traies la char corrumpue au desoz,	stretch the head so you draw the rotten skin underneath,
et descuevre la char sus le leu ou tu vues soier, que li soie ne blece la char;	uncover the skin on the place where you wish to be, let the skin not blister the char.
et met .i. tison ou une tauble desoz l’os por mues coper la char corrumpue;	And put [something like] a splint or a board beneath the bone to cover the decayed flesh.
et covient tant soier com on puet veoir et sentir la corruption, et soier ancor autre fois.	It must be as much as can be seen and felt of the corruption, and also be checked again.
Et se li os est corrumpus, et n’apert mie, et li corruptions est en mileu ou en une partie,	If the bone is rotten and does not open, and the corruption is in the middle or a part of it,
si descuevre la char toute; puis met .i. tison desoz,	If the decayed flesh is exposed, put [something like] a splint underneath,
et puis soie des l’une partie a l’autre la corruption, et soit li soieure dou lonc de la corruption .i. poc, si com nos avons dit;	And then, from one part to another, there should be corruption, and the length of the corruption shall be a finger, as we have said;
et se li corruptions est en la jointure, si cope la jointure corrumpue, et soie l’os ou elle contient de l’autre part;	If the corruption is at the joint, strike the corrupt joint and break the bone on the other side of it;
et se li corruptions est en la continuation des .ij. jointes, si n’i a autre angien que dou coper;	And if the corruption is in the continuity of two joints, there is no remedy but to crush it;
et se li corruptions est ou poignil de la main, ou ou poignil dou piet, si est mout fort celle chose,	And if the corruption is at the hilt of the hand or foot, this is a serious matter,
mais toutevoie il covient que tu enquieres celle corrosion, coment elle t’apert;	But always it is necessary that you investigate that corruption, how it opens.
et la mundifie en toutes les manieres que tu pues, mais que li voine ou li nerf ne te faicent contraire;	and clean it in all ways that you can, but do not let the vein or the nerve harm you.
et saiches que li incisoire et les soies por coper ces os sont maintes, selonc l’assise des os et l’aparance d’ous,	and know that there are many saws and files to cut these bones according to their placement and the appearance of them.
et lor grossece et lor subtiliteit, et lor grandor et lor petitece, et lor duresce;	and their thickness and thinness, their largeness and smallness, and their hardness;
et por ceu covient il apareillier a chescune semblance d’ovraige son estrument;	And because, it is necessary to equip for every kind of operation, its tool.
et saiches que l’uevre te moustrera l’estrument dont tu avras mestier, selonc la conissance de cest art,	Know that the operation will show you the tool that you need, according to the knowledge of this art.
et le tesmoignaige des manieres des maladies;	and the testimony of the ways of diseases;
si porpense l’estrument dont tu as mestier selonc ceu qu’il le covient.	if you consider the tool that you need, according to what is required.
dou feu	hot fire
Li chiés porrissent ou par cause dedens, ou par cause defuer;	The head may burst open from within or due to pressure.
et quant tu avras medicinee celle corrosion par la cure des medicines, et il ne profitent mie,	and when you have applied the corrosive treatment using medicines but it does not help,
si covient coper celui membre jusques au leu ou li corrosion vient,	if it is necessary to cover that member up to the level where the corrosion occurs,
si que li malaides eschaipe par ceu de la mort, ou par la malice, qui est plus grans, de la defaute dou membre;	If the patient is scorched by this (cautery), it may lead to death or a greater evil, which is the damage to the member.
et li signes si est que li membres devient noir, si qu’il semble qu’il soit ars dou feu,	And the signs are that the limb becomes black as if it were burned by fire.
et porrist aprés la noiror, puis va celle corrosions de membre em membre,	And afterwards comes blackness followed by the corrosion of the member to member,
et prent par tout le cors; si te haste dou coper,	And takes hold of the whole body; if you hurry to cover it.
et se c’est par la percussion d’aucunes venimouses bestes, si com scorpion de mer et wivre et semblans,	and if it is by the sting of some poisonous animals like sea scorpions, vipers, and similar,
se li corrosion est au chief dou doi, si le cope, et ne li doner mie espaice de venir jusc’a la main.	if the corruption is at the head of the tooth, cover it, and give it no space to come up to the hand.
Et s’elle vient jusc’a la main, si la cope a la jointe, si que la corrosion ne viegne jusc’a bras;	And if it comes up to the wrist, strike at the joint so that the corruption does not reach the arm.
et s’elle vient au bras, si le cope au coute; et s’elle passe le coute, c’est li mors,	If it reaches the elbow, strike at the joint; if it goes beyond the elbow, it is death.
et n’i vaut amenistremens fuers que li quantitez de sa vertut;	and nothing else should be used except for the quantity of its strength.
et tot ensi fai quant li corrosion vient ou piet: s’elle vient en la premiere jointe, si la cope aprés l’autre jointe;	and so do as follows when corruption or pus arrives: if it comes in the first joint, strike after the other joint.
et s’elle vient ou piet, si cope tout le piet;	And if it comes or falls, strike the whole fall.
et s’elle monte en la jambe, si cope a la jointure dou genoil;	If it rises in the leg, strike at the knee joint.
et s’elle vient desus le genoil, si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier le malaide a mort;	If it comes above the knee, there is no other device for the patient except to kill him.
et li maniere dou coper ou dou soier le membre si est que tu le lie desus et desoz,	And the manner to cover or to dress a limb is such that you bind it above and below.
et estende uns menistres l’un des liiens aval, et uns autres ministres l’autre liien amont,	And stretch one minister one of the lower cords, and another minister the other cord above.
et tu dessevre la char qui est entre les .ij. liiens a .i. spatumile large, tant que li os soit descovers;	and you separate the flesh that is between the two cords about one thumb's width wide, so that the bone is exposed.
puis le cope ou soie, et met de chescune part .i. drapeil de lin, si que li soie ne touche le leu sain,	then cover or dress it, and place a linen cloth on each side, so that the dressing does not touch healthy flesh.
et viegne au malaide autre lesion et aposteme chaus.	And comes to the patient another injury and abscesses swollen.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient quant tu oevres, si cauterize le leu hastanment,	And if bleeding comes when you work, then cauterize the place immediately.
ou tu met sus aucunes poudres restraignans; puis revien a ta medicine tant qu’elle soit acomplie,	or put some powders restraining on it; then return to your medicine until it is accomplished,
puis lie le membre navreit d’un liien covenauble, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then bind the limb with a removable ligature, and cure it until it heals;
et je te conterai k’il avint a .i. home en som piet:	And I will tell you what happens to a man lying on his side:
il li avint une noiror qui sembloit arsure de feu,	there comes a blackness that looks like a burn by fire,
et celle corrosion vint premier en son doi dou piet, tant qu’elle porprist tout le piet;	and this corrosion began first in his lower back, until it consumed all the lower back;
et quant li hons vit la corrosion, si se hasta de coper le piet, et fut sanez;	And when the horse sees corrosion, it pierces its hoof with copper and becomes clean;
et lonc tens aprés li revint li corrosion ou doi de la main, et il vint a moi,	And for a long time after that, the corrosion or pus comes back again from his hand, and it came to me,
et je li mis sus choses repercussives aprés la mundification dou cors, et ne pot cesser li corrosions;	and I put him on things that would reflect after the cleansing of the body, but the corrosion could not stop.
et il vot que je li copasse la main, et je ne vou, que je avoie esperance de repercuter la matiere;	and I said that I would cut his hand off, and I did not want to unless I had hope of reflection (of the disease).
et doutai ausi que se je tailloie sa main, qu’il ne morist,	And also he doubts if I am to cut his hand, that he will not die.
car li vertus de l’ome estoit foible; et il se despera toz, et revint en sa terre,	for the virtue of man was weak; and he gave up all hope, and returned to his land,
et se hasta de coper sa main, et fut sanez;	and struck her with a sword on the hand, and she was well.
et je n’ai ceu conteit fuers que por ceu c’on faice autreteil, s’on en a mestier.	and I have not heard this story for any other reason than that it is used when it is necessary.
Aucune fois vient aposteme en leu charnut, et demore si longement qu’il fait grant assemblee de bowe;	An abscess sometimes appears in a charred place, and stays so long that it causes a large swelling of boils.
et puis ront et perce, et en saut li bowe, et demoure li leus vuis, ausi com uns vasselz;	Then they run and pierce, causing the boil to burst, and the wound remains open like a wound of a soldier.
et li cuir qui est desus est ausi subtilz com .i. drapelz deliiez,	and the skin that is above is as thin as one layer of linen cloth.
et ne corront mie jusc’a l’os, ne jusc’au nerf, et telz maladie si est apelee «sain»,	and they do not pierce all the way to the bone or to the nerve, and such disease is called "sain".
et n’est mie apelee «fistule»;	And is not called "fistula".
mais s’elle est si alongie qu’elle viegne jusc’a l’os em parfont, si est apelee «fistule»;	But if it extends so much that it reaches the bone entirely, it is called "fistula";
et li cuire si est que tu cope celui cuir tout entor, et meismement quant il est subtilz, ausi com uns drapelz;	And the cure is that you cut through the entire hide, as well as when it is subtle, just like a cloth.
et ne s’aert mie por sa corruption.	and does not heal due to its corruption.
Et se tu as fiance que li cuirs s’aerde, et li corruption n’est mie en parfont,	And if you have suspicion that the flesh is hardened, and the corruption is not complete,
et li cuir est espés de char, si le cure de clistere ensi:	and the skin is thick with pus, cure it with cleansing in this way:
regarde se li seins est grans, et li bowe qui en ist est de puant odor,	check if the breasts are large, and the boil which is there is of bad smell,
adonques le clisterize de medicine egiptiaine qui est ensi faite:	Then cleanse it with Egyptian medicine which is made in this way:
prenez aisil, et oile, et litargire, igalment, et metez cuire en .i. vassel au feu,	Take asafetida, oil, and liquiritiga, equally, and cook in one vessel over the fire.
tant que li medicine soit rouge, et deviegne ausi espesse com miel;	until the medicine is red, and becomes as thick as honey;
et puis pren de ceu selonc ta necessiteit, et le font en aigue et en miel,	and then take from this according to your need, and make it into an oil and honey mixture.
et en clisterize lou sein, et estraint le pertus;	and apply as a poultice to the breast, and constrict the hernia.
et laisse la medicine ens par .ij. houres, puis l’estrai en espreignant;	And let the medicine remain for 2 hours, then extract it gently.
fai ce mout de fois, tant que li seins soit mondefiiez, et soit ostee li puor;	Do this several times until the breast is softened and the pus is removed.
et aucune fois est clisterizeis d’aigue de cendres,	And at one time it is cleaned with water of ashes,
quant ceste medicine n’est presens, et est que tu preignes cendres de fust de vigne, et giete aigue desus,	when this medicine is not present, then you take vine ash and pour water over it,
puis la coule, et en clisterize, tant que tu saiches que li seins est bien mondez;	Then clean it and anoint with ointment, until you know that the breast is healed.
et se li malaides ne le puet soffrir, ne la medicine egiptiaine ne l’aigue de cendres,	if the patient cannot bear it, nor the Egyptian medicine nor ash water,
si le clisterize d’aigue et de miel ou il ait un poc de litargire broiet;	if the anointment is made of water and honey or has a little litharge powdered.
ou tu la clistirize de miel et de vin melleit, que li mielz ait proprieteit de mundifiier et de laver,	or you anoint with honey and sweet wine, as the honey has properties to purify and wash,
et li vins fait aerdre le sain;	and the wine makes the wound heal.
et quant tu as ce fait, et tu as fiance que li seins est bien mundifiiez,	and when you have done this, and you are certain that the wound is well cleaned,
si le clisterize de ceu que fait naistre char en li,	if you anoint with that which causes pus to form in it,
et est que tu preignes emplaustre diafinit, et le font avec oile roset et en vin;	And you are to take a plaster made definite, and make it with rose oil and wine.
ou tu le clisterize d’aucunes medicines et d’oignemens, dont j’ai dit les proprietez ou traitier des oignemens;	and you anoint [the wound or affected area] with some medicines and ointments, as I have said the properties for treating sores.
et se li pertus dou sein est petis, et li cainne dou clistere n’i puet entrer,	if the sore on the breast is small, and the size of the plaster cannot enter it.
si l’eslarge d’un fer un poc, et met ens une tente de l’oignement egiptiein,	if the wound is about a thumb's width, cover it with an Egyptian ointment tent.
ou oignement basilicon, tant k’il soit eslargiez;	Apply basilicon ointment, when it is diluted.
et se li plaie est trop large, si la cout et i laisse tant soulement .i. leu ou li clistere puisse entrer,	and if the wound is too wide, cut it to allow at least one league or the cautery to enter.
et se li pertus que giete bowe est au desus, si le cope ou plus bas leu que i est.	and if the ulcer that bows out is above, strike or hit it lower than where it is.
Car quant li bowe est en parfont, si n’i laisse enjanrer char;	For when the boil is fully formed, do not let any flesh grow into it.
et se tu ne pues coper lou sein desoz si com tu vues,	And if you cannot cover the chest beneath as you see,
si appareille en tel maniere que li bowe corre au plus bas leu que i est,	then arrange it in such a way that the belly presses at its lowest point.
car quant li bowe est parfont, si n’i laisse enjanrer char	because when the belly is full, do not allow any air to enter it.
et se tu ne pues coper lou sein desoz si com tu vues,	et si tu le vois li bowe se tressorbe et s’il est mouilli de moisteur,
si apareille en teil maniere: que li bowe corre legierement aval, et n’i lassier rien de la bowe;	If it appears in such a manner: that the thigh bone slides slightly downward, and leaves nothing of the thigh.
et pren medicines consolidatives por mettre sor le sein,	and take medicines for strengthening to place on the breast.
et estent sus .i. drapeil de lin que cuevre tout le sein;	and cover it with one linen cloth that covers the entire breast.
puis cope as forces endroit le pertus dou sein .i. poc plus large dou premier,	Then apply force to the chest wound, which is slightly larger than the first one.
pues estent oignement souef sus .i. autre drapel selonc la quantiteit dou pertus,	Then apply anointment (ointment or salve) on top of the other bandage according to the size of the wound.
et le met sus le pertus dou sein por aligier la bowe, et n’oster mie le grant drapeil fuers que aprés maint jor une fois;	and place it on the chest wound to align the ribs, but do not remove the large bandage for several days.
et celui qui est sor le pertus dou sein, oste sovent por oster la bowe,	and he who is over the chest wound, removes it frequently to remove the ribs.
et saiches ceu que corra de la bowe, se c’est venin ou poc ou assez, ou digeste, ou indigeste;	And know what runs from the bowel, whether it is poison or food, or digested, or indigestible.
et pren warde se li patiens sent dolor ou nom, et s’il i a aposteme ou non,	and take care if the patient feels pain or not, and if there is an abscess or not,
et quant ta medicine s’est en teil maniere estendue et tu vois la nature que saut sus le pertus dou sein,	and when your medicine has been spread in this manner and you see the nature that rises above the breast bone,
si saiches que li seins s’aert ja, et aproche li santez;	If you know that the breast is hard, approach the healthy ones.
et puis le deslie le matin, ou le tier jor, et quant tu delies la plaie,	And then dislocate it in the morning or at midday, and when you dislocate the wound,
si chainge .i. autre drapeil, et renovele l’oignement.	then change one bandage and renew the ointment.
Et se li seins giete bowe indigeste aprés maint jor, saiches que li seins ne s’aert mie.	And if the breast falls inward improperly after many days, know that the breast does not heal itself.
Et se venins subtilz cort aprés lonc tens, si ne te desperer mie de la santeit,	And if subtle poison courts for a long time, do not despair of health,
car li santez aproche. Car il i a homes cui tarde enjanremens de char en ses plaies, et de ces que font le contraire;	For the health approaches. Because there are men whose wounds delay healing, and of those who do the opposite;
et se bowe indigeste saut dou sein aprés maint jor, saiches que li seins ne s’aert mie;	and if it swells indigestedly after many days, know that the breasts will not heal.
et se li seins tarde d’aerdre, et est porloigniez, si ajoste medicines sechans moistes en substance et seches en vertut,	and if the breasts swell and are hardened, use drying medicines that are moist in substance and dry in effect.
si com oignement diafinit, car il i a grant partie de vitriole, et c’est li derriene medicine;	As with an egg shell, for it contains much vitriol, and it is the last remedy;
pren oignement dyafinit, et le font avec oile roset, et l’arose de viel vin igal en substance;	Take an egg-shell made defined, make it with rose oil, and mix it with equal parts of old wine in substance;
puis le confit et en use; et ceu meisme fait mielz cuit engroissiez,	then cook and use it; and the same thing is better cooked thickened,
quant oignemens dyafinit n’est presens,	when egg-shells are not present,
ou tu pren mirre et aloen et encens, et le broie, et le poudre sus le miel quant il est sor le feu;	Take myrrh, aloe, and incense, grind them together, and sprinkle the powder on honey when it is over the fire.
et puis en glue .i. drapel, et l’estent sor le sein, et aucune fois i aministre on aristologe longe,	Then place one cloth, and set it on the chest, and once in a while administer an aristolochia leaf.
et racines de lis celeste, qui est ausi com farine de veces et centoire;	and roots of celestial lily, which is like flour and centory sometimes.
et en use de simples ou de compostes: broie les, et en fai poudre, et met sus le miel que j’ai dit, et en use;	and in the use of simple or compound remedies: grind them, make powder, and sprinkle on the honey as I said, and use.
et se li cure est alongie, et n’est curez par ceste cure,	And if the patient is healthy and not treated by this cure,
adonc saiches que la corruptions est em parfont, et fait empression en l’os, ou as membres durs, ou as liemens;	Therefore, know that corruption occurs throughout [the body], causing pressure on the bones or hard parts, or the ligaments;
si le cure de la cure de fistule, si com nos avons dit ci devant.	if the cure of the fistula cure, as we have said before.
de l’aposteme de l’ungle	of the abscess on the nail bed.
Panarice est un aposteme que naist desoz l’ungle dou pouchiet de la main,	Pouches of the hand give rise to an abscess called Pararice.
ou dou piet, ou par aventure naist en autres dois;	or it can arise near the foot, or by chance in other places;
et quant il est envielliez, et on n’i prent garde, si i vient .i. aposteme chaus,	and when it becomes swollen and no care is taken, one abscess grows there.
et corront et giete bowe tant qu’elle corront la racine de l’ungle, et par aventure la corront toute;	And they will run and throw arrows until they reach the root of the nail, and by chance, they may hit it all.
et vient li corrosions jusc’a l’os, tant qu’il i vient dolor puant, et est li chiés dou doi larges, et est li color fuxe.	Then comes the corrosion up to the bone, until it brings painful smell, and the shoulder is wide open, and the color turns black.
Quant tu le cures si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie,	When you treat it as we have said in the section, but the treatment does not help.
si covient que tu copes a i. fer toute la superfluiteit qui est demoree de l’ungle,	Therefore, you should cut off the entire superfluous part that remains of the nail.
puis cauterize la plaie aprés.	Then cauterize the wound after.
Li cauteres est mout grans aide se li os est sains, et li ungle est sainne;	The cautery is very helpful if the bone is healthy and the nail is healthy;
et se li ungle apresse la char ens, et l’encomence a poindre, et la blece,	and if the nail grows into the flesh and begins to itch, and swell;
si covient que tu mettes lou rait desoz l’ungle que point la char,	then you must put the medicine under the nail to prevent the flesh from growing;
et la boute en haut, et cope celi char subtilment et legierement,	And raise it up, and strike the flesh gently and softly.
et met sus le remenant de la char medicines ardans et corrosives por oster tout;	and put on top of the remaining flesh the remnants of the burning and corrosive medicine to remove everything.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then cure it with herbs until it is healed.
Et se li corrosion est en l’os, si le cope, et trai fuer, car tant com li os corrumpus i est, si ne puet saner;	If the corrosion is in the bone, strike and pull out, as the more the bone is corrupted, the less it can heal.
et se tu vois le doi corrumpre, si le cope en .i. des nous si com il est devant dit,	And if you see the two (bones) to be misaligned, strike them with a hammer as previously stated,
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then let it heal while it is clean;
et s’il est ferus, et boutez, et il sent grant dolor, si covient que tu le sainnes premier;	and if it is injured, lance it, and it causes great pain, then you must first let it drain.
puis cope l’ungle dou spatumile agut en taillant de travers desus,	then strike the angle of the humerus bone with a sharp tool in a cutting motion from above.
et warde que li taille ne viegne jusc’a la char qui est desoz l’ungle, car li malaides sentiroit trop grant dolor;	And watch that the tip (of the instrument) does not reach the flesh that is beneath the nail, for the patient would feel too great pain.
et s’il avient, si met chose sus qui apaise.	If it happens, put something on it to soothe.
la dolor dou sourdoit de la main	the pain in the deaf hand
Li dois ajostez qui naist en mains d’aucuns homes par aventure est toz charnus,	The boils that arise on some men's hands by chance are all fleshy.
et par aventure i a teil ou il a osses, et aucune fois i a ungle,	And by chance it has teeth or bones, and sometimes it has nails,
et aucun d’aus naissent en la racine de la jointure, ou li naissance est en aucuns nous des dois.	And any of them grow at the root of the joint, or the growth occurs in some of the fingers.
Cil qui naist en aucune nout dou doi ne se muet,	The one that grows in a knuckle on the finger does not move,
et cil qui naist a la jointure dou doi, par aventure se muet;	And the one that grows at the joint of the finger may move (or stop moving).
la taille de celui qui est charnus si est legiere, en teil maniere:	The belly of a fat person is light in this way:
taille le en sa racine d’un large spatumile.	The belly of a fat person is light in this way: its root should be probed with a wide spatula.
Cil qui naist en la racine de la jointure si est grief a curer: si te tien dou coper.	If it is born in the root of the joint, it is difficult to cure; hold it covered.
En celui qui naist ou doit au derrien nout, si covient que tu copes premier la char reondement jusc’a l’os,	In one who is born or about to die, you must cut the round flesh up to the bone first.
puis cope l’os a une soie convenable a ceu, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then cut the bone with an appropriate saw for that, and cure it until it is healed.
Li soudemens que vient as dois ensamble vient par naissance, ou par soudement de plaie, ou par arsure de feu, ou par semblans choses.	The swelling that comes at the joints happens at the same time by birth, or by injury of a wound, or by burning with fire, or by similar things.
Si couvient que tu copes celle soudeure, si que li doit repairent selonc lor formes naturelz;	It is necessary to cut the swelling so that it can repair according to its natural forms;
puis met entre dous tentes ou drapelz moilliez en oile roset, qu’il ne se soudent;	Then place between two tents or dampened cloths oiled with rose oil, so that they do not stick.
ou tu met entre dous pieces de plonc subtilz, tant que li leus soit soudez, si com il covient.	and you place between two thin wooden boards until the edges are glued, as required.
Se soudemens vient a aucun de ses dois avec la paume, si cope celle sodure si com il covient.	If one of its sides comes with the palm, then strike that joint as required.
Des vils	The poor
Vis sont voinnes grosses envoloupees pleines de superfluitez melancoliouses, que vienent em plusors membres dou cors;	The veins are large, swollen, filled with melancholic superfluidities, which come in many members of the body.
et plus avient en jambes de ces qui vont a piet et qui travaillent et portent, que a autres.	And it happens more in legs of those who walk and work and carry, than in others.
Il covient donques que tu li aministres aucune fois espurgement de cole, et puis le saine de la basilique.	Therefore, you must administer purge of gall, and then the healthy from the basilica.
Li cure de fer si est selonc .ij. manieres: l’une est c’on les cope, et traie on fuer le sanc noir;	The iron cure is according to two ways: one is when they are struck, and black blood is drained out;
et li autre maniere si est que tu lieves la voinne, et la trai toute fuer.	And another way is that you open the vein and draw it out completely.
Li taille si est selonc ceste maniere: arose li premier la jambe d’aigue chaude mout fort, tant que li gros sans soit subtiliiez,	The incision method is as follows: first stretch the leg with very hot sharp iron, until the flesh is softened,
puis estrain la jambe dou malaide des desus la cuixe jusc’a la partie desoz le genoil;	Then bind the leg of the patient from above the calf to below the knee;
puis cope la voinne en .i. leu, ou en .ij. ou en .iij., d’une taille large,	Then open the vein in one place, or two, or three, of a large size,
puis eslieve et trair fuer le sanc noir a ta main, des l’un chief jusc’a l’autre, tant que tant de sans en isse com li vertus dou malaide puet soffrir;	Then slice and drain the black blood from your hand to the other, as much blood as the disease in the patient can bear.
et puis la lie, et li comande qu’il se teigne de viandes enjanrant cole noire;	and then bind it up, and command him to fast on black meat for a while.
et recomence l’evacuation et la sainie quant les voinnes sont plainnes, et nuist au malaide.	and repeat the evacuation and purification when the veins are full, which benefits the patient.
Li alevemens de li est selonc ceste maniere: reis la jambe dou malaide, s’il i a mout de poil,	The swellings of it (the patient) are as follows: stretch the leg of the patient, if there is much hair on it,
puis le met ou bain, et li. arose la jambe d’aigue chaude tant qu’elle deviegne rouge, et enflent les voinnes;	then place it in water and let (the leg) rise from warm hot water until it turns red and the veins swell;
et se tu n’as point de baing, si le chaufe au feu, et puis le cope endroit la voinne dou lonc au chief dou genoil, ou en la partie desoz a la cheville;	and if you do not have water, heat it in the fire, and then press it against the vein along the length of the thigh or in the part below the ankle;
puis aoevre le cuir a l’oncine, et escorche la voinne de chescune part, tant qu’ele apere quant on la sent;	then peel the skin around it, and cut open the vein from both sides, until it appears when you feel it;
et on la voit rouge et noire, et quant elle entre ou cuir si semble ausi com une corde blainche;	And one sees it red and black, and when it enters or skin appears as if a white cord;
puis boute le rait desoz, tant qu’ele soit alevee dou cuir, et puis la pent a l’oncine legier,	Then push the rod beneath, until it is raised from the skin, and then prick it lightly at an angle.
puis le cope en .i. autre leu ensus iij. dois; puis escorche le cuir sus la voinne tant qu’ele apere,	Then strike it in another place nearby four fingers; then scrape the skin over the vein as far as it appears,
puis la lieve au rais, si com tu as fait, et la pent a un autre uncine, si com tu as fait premiers;	Then lift the rod as you have done, and prick it at another angle, as you did before;
puis cope une autre taille, ou plusors se tu en as mestier, puis la lieve, et la cope au doi dou piet,	Then take another size, or more if needed, then heat it, and apply it to the base of the foot.
puis la trai et lieve jusc’a la seconde taille; puis l’estrai de taille en taille, tant qu’elle isse toute fuer, puis la cope;	Then draw and heat it up to the second size; then file it down by size until it is entirely red hot, then apply it.
et se tu ne la pues traire et lever, si i boute une aguille a tout .i. fil fort double,	and if you cannot draw it out and lift it, push an awl with thick, strong wire through it.
et la lie et la trai, et i boute desoz .i. rait, et torne ta main d’une part et d’autre, tant qu’il en isse;	And pull and tug, and push something underneath it (the dislocation), and turn your hand from one side to the other until it comes out.
et garde qu’elle ne cope, car s’elle cope, si ne la puet on traire ne lever, et en vient nuisement au malaide;	And ensure that it does not break, for if it breaks, one cannot pull or lift it, and this would harm the patient.
et quant tu l’as toute traite, si met sor le leu de la plaie laine moillie en vin et en oile roset; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you have treated it (the dislocation), place on the wound of the injury linen soaked in wine and rose oil, and treat it until it heals.
Et se li vis est contraite et torte et envoloupee ensamble, et ele n’est mie droite, si com nos avons dit,	If the vision is constricted, twisted and swollen together, and it is not straight as we have said,
si covient que tu la fendes tortement, mais ne la coper mie; et la trai si com nos avons devant dit.	If you must cut it, do so crookedly, but do not cover it; drag it as we have said before.
Li forme dou fer dont on cope la vis si est corbes, et ne trenche mie, qu’il ne cope la voinne;	The shape of the iron used to pierce the vein should be curved and not sharp, so as not to cut the vein;
et est de grosse corbeure, car s’il estoit subtilz, si coperoit la voine, mais soit gros si com nos avons dit, et ci est li forme:	and should be large, because if it is too thin, it will pierce the vein; however, it should be thick as we have said, and this is its shape:
De la voinne civile	The vein of the body
Ceste voinne est enjanree en jambes, en chaudes parties ou il ne naist herbes ne arbre, et en terre ou il n’a point de moistor;	This vein is located in the legs, in warm places where no plants or trees grow, and in dry ground without moisture.
et par aventure naist autre part qu’en jambes, et ceu avient de la porriture que vient desoz le cuir,	And it may happen elsewhere than in the legs, which is due to rotting coming from under the skin.
si com il vient dedens le cors serpens et vers, enjanrez entre cuir et char.	As it comes within the body snakes and worms, locate the vein between the skin and flesh.
Et se li signes de l’encomencement de ceste voinne si est qu’il vient en la jambe une tres grans enflammation,	If the signs of the beginning of this vein are that it comes in the leg with a very large inflammation,
puis se chainge li leus, et comence li voinne fors issir, ausi com une racine d’une plante.	Then change the joints, and start the vein to open out, just like a root of a plant.
Quant li chiés apert, si covient que tu envoloupes entor une piece de plonc des une З et demi jusc’a .ij. З., et la noe,	When the head (of a limb) opens up, it is necessary that you tie around a piece of wood from 1 and a half to 2 cubits (in circumference), and sew it.
et laisse le plonc pendant a la jambe, et totes les fois qu’il en ist point au defuer, si l’envoloupe entor le plonc, et la nowe;	and leave the wood (in place), and every time it begins to swell, re-tie around the wood and sew.
et s’elle est trop longe, si en cope une partie, et envoloupe le remenant, et ne la coper mie en sa racine, tant qu’elle soit toute issue;	If it is too long (the dislocated limb), cut a part of it and wrap the remaining, do not cover it at its root, until it is all out.
car se tu la copes, si rentre en la char, et fait venir aposteme et porriture ou leu, et male maladie;	If you cut it (the dislocated limb), it will return into the flesh, cause an abscess and putrefaction or illness.
por la queil chose il covient qu’elle soit traite poc et poc jusc’a chief, et n’en remaigne rien ou cors;	Therefore, it is necessary to treat it bit by bit until the head (the end) remains, and nothing in the body.
et est aucune fois ceste voinne quant elle est traite de .v. paumes de lonc, ou de .x.,	Sometimes this vein when treated measures from five to ten fingers long.
et uns hons vint ja a moi, a cui elle issit de .x. paumes de long, et quant tu la copes, si boute .i. rais ou pertus, et la perce jusc’a fons,	And once a man came to me, whose [shoulder] was ten fingers long, and when you cut it open, press it with one pound or pounded iron, and pierce it to the bottom,
si que tout en isse; et soit vuidie li matiere qui est dedens, et amenistre au leu medicines enjanrans porriture aucun jor, puis le cure si com les apostemes.	and let everything come out of it; empty the matter that is inside, and bring in medicines for rotting wounds every day, then treat it as an abscess.
Et aucune fois a ceste voinne mains rains, et meismement quant elle apert en la jointure dou piet, ou ou piet,	And sometimes at this vein, many hands are placed, and especially when it opens at the joint of the foot or the ankle,
et i vient mout de pertus, et dont il saut rains; cure le donques si com nos avons dit devant.	And it often comes about with wounds, from which blood flows profusely; treat it then as we have said before.
Des vers qui naissent entre cuir et char	From the worms that are born between skin and flesh.
Ceste maladie est apelee en nostre terre «maladie de buef», por ceu qu’elle avient maintes fois as bués,	This disease is called "cattle disease" in our land, because it often occurs in cattle,
et est un petis vers qui naist entre cuir et char, et va par tout le cors montant et dessendant,	It is a small worm that is born between skin and flesh, which travels through the entire body swelling and descending,
et le sent om bien a l’aler de membre en membre, tant qu’il desront le cuir ou il vait, et saut fuer;	and he feels it well when moving from member to member, until he tears the skin or jumps away;
et est enjanrez de porriture d’aucunes humors, si com vienent vers et serpens et lumbris et ascarides ou ventre;	and is burned by pustules of certain humors, such as those that come towards worms, snakes, lizards and ascarids (worms) in the belly;
et doute on de son malice, car quant il va par le cors, et il monte au chief, et il vient a l’oil,	and one doubts his malice, for when he goes through the body, and it rises to the head, and comes to the eye,
par aventure rentre, et destruit l’oil; et ceu avient maintes fois.	by chance enters and destroys the eye; and this happens many times.
Quant tu le vues curer et traire, si ne puet on fuers que quant il vait:	When you see it to cure and draw, one can force it out only when it goes:
si covient donques que tu lies le leu desus et desoz d’un fort liien bien estroitement,	Then you must bind the joint above and below with a strong rope tightly.
puis cope sus et le trai fuer, et se li vers est em parfont en la char, et tu ne le trueves,	Then you must cut off above and draw out thoroughly, and if its head is embedded in the flesh, you must not pull it.
si le cauterize de feu sus, tant qu’il muire;	If you cauterize with fire, until it dies;
et li plus grans nuisemens que il fait, si est qu’il corront l’oil, si com nos avons dit;	and the greatest harm that it causes is that it burns oil, as we have said;
et se tu le vois venir ou chief pres de l’oil, si estraint desoz lui le sorcil forment, puis cope sus, et le trai fuer;	and if you see it coming or near the oil, squeeze the scourge under it, then strike above it and pull it out.
et covient user le malaide de mundifiement de cors de medicines solutives por les males humors porries,	and the patient must be treated with purifying body medicine for dissolving evil humors.
et se warse de viandes enjanrans porriture.	And if boils from spoiled meat burst.
De la dolor qui vient de ventositeit	Of the pain that comes from wind-inflammation
Ceste maladie est apelee en nostre terre «vakirir», et est une dolor que vient en aucuns membres,	This disease is called in our land "whitered", and it is a pain that comes in some members,
et pues se mue de membre en membre; et je vis ceu que je vos di.	and then it moves from member to member; and I have seen this which I tell you.
