Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne .i. liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is at its furthest point, let the patient lie down, as we have said in the one who has sciatica, and stretch out one tie on the sick leg properly, and also on the thigh.
puis met .ij. tisons, .i. au chief et .i. autre as piez, puis fiche .i. tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	Then place two splinters, one at the neck and one at the feet, then insert one splinter between the thighs of the patient in the shape of a cross.
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	And place damp cloths around it to prevent the patient from bleeding, then extend each of the assistants towards him, and the surgeon should hold the dislocation equal to his hand.
S’elle revient, c’est boin. Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If it comes back into place, that's good. Otherwise, lay him on a table, press as we have said in the dislocation, and make the patient lie on the healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit; et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	And when there is a dislocation in front (of the body), it is necessary to stretch the affected leg immediately, and as I have said; and the surgeon should be on top of the injured angle, then press with the other hand, and pull downward towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les .ij. hainches;	And if the dislocation is towards the outside, it should not be extended downwards, nor lifted up from the ground, but it should remain as when a person is dislocated in the same way as we have said about lying on the two hips;
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	and it should be on its face, and the limb extended as we have said before, and pressure should be applied to the joint on the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz; adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	and it will be in place when the patient extends his legs, and they are even; then adjust the knees, apply the splint, and fasten it with a bandage so that the hip does not move;
et se repose .iij. jors ou .iiij., puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus; et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse. iij. jors; puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And it rests for three or four days, then dislocate and place the splint over it; if you see they are even, tighten, as before, and leave it. Three days; then dislocate, and make it move well, until the limb is comforted.
de la dislocation dou genoil	On the dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc .iij. manieres: c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier; et ne desalue point devant.	The knee can be dislocated in four ways: inside, outside, and backward; but not forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the signs are that you instruct the patient to bend their leg at the knee, and if it does not bend at the knee, know that it is dislocated.
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	And the restoration is that you have the patient sit upright, and extend their leg if they can, and place your back on their front, and place their foot on your feet.
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les .ij. costez dou genoil forment; et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	Then take hold of their knee with both hands and pull apart the two sides of the knee, forming it into a V shape. Have another attendant extend their foot until the knee returns to its place, and the signs are that it bends at the knee lightly.
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort .iij. jors ou iiij., puis le deslie; et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And apply the plaster on top, and make the leg stretched from the knee to the ankle, and leave them joined firmly for 3 or 4 days, then release it; and do not let the patient walk until the limbs are comforted.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the limbs are not straight, then provide strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the hernia, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	of the ankle dislocation
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are sometimes swollen, and sometimes completely dislocated, both within and outwardly.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And the signs are that the ankle is swollen, and it bends forward towards the part where it is dislocated:
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	The reduction (resetting) is easy, and it should be done gently when only swollen.    Here comes the translation of the next line:
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne .i. ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when the dislocation is complete (total), you must make the patient sit straight, and hold one minister on either side of the leg above the ankle:   Translation:
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre .ij. fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	Then pull the foot towards you with your right hand, and then towards your left hand twice, then stretch it upwards, and push the foot upwards forcefully.
et fai ce .ij. fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	and do this twice as we have said, pushing and pulling the foot; if it returns, that is good; if not, repeat the work, for it will return.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche .i. passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	and if it cannot return in this way, place the patient on his back on the ground, and make a firm stab into the ground between his legs, and tie rags around it so that it does not cut the patient.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a .i. liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	Then the ministers anoint the thigh, and another minister extends the foot to its limits or to the knee, so that it lies above the foot on the neck.
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	Then all ministers extend equally, and the patient's legs should be close together between the thighs to hold the patient when stretching him.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	Then place the mirrors equally on the dislocation in their hands, and another minister anoints the healthy leg beneath, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it is at the correct point, place the plaster and wadding on top, form it, and tie the foot to the leg. Be careful of the nerves that are behind the ankle, make sure the bindings are not too tight.
puis le laisse .ij. jors ou .iij., et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par .iiij. jors;	Let it be left for two or three days, and if the ligaments soften, hold them together; then release it on the third or fourth day, and order the patient to rest for four days.
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	If it goes before that term, it is not certain that it will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If an abscess has come to a head, then you must open it, as we have said elsewhere, until it is healed.
des dois	of the hands
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the fingers are dislocated, they should be carefully stretched out without strain, and it is an easy thing.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus .i. leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is on the back of the hand or foot, you must make the patient sit on a flat surface or table, and put your foot above where those joints open, then press your foot firmly until it returns to its place.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a .ij. chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse .iij. jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and when it is equal and there is no opening, you put two fingers under the foot's sole, then apply pressure and leave it for four hours, then release it; let it rest until it heals.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	Of wounds and dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound occurs along with dislocation, and it is attempted to be restored, many times the patient dies.
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	do not be presumptuous in the treatment, unless you are wise in the art and have long experience with it, and if you are not compassionate and merciful and patient, do not be bold.
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	and at the beginning, you should use a warm poultice for an abscess, and leave the patient in the hands of God if you see no hope of health.
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	And when you see hope, then reset the limb to its place, so that the abscess closes.
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	And when the limb is in place, administer remedies to soothe the abscess, heal the wound, as needed, with ointments of a drying nature.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if there is a dislocation with a fracture and small bones are displaced, set the bones, and do as we have said for simple diseases.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors. Amen	And keep yourself from entering into fear, according to what I have said, for it will harm you according to your Creator, and because of the knowledge of your weapons and body. Amen
